It coordinates health checks across three endpoints:\n\n- **healthz**: Legacy endpoint for backwards compatibility\n- **livez**: Liveness probe that can have a grace period during startup\n- **readyz**: Readiness probe with no grace period\n\n## Key Features\n\n**Grace Period Support**: The implementation allows livez checks to have a configurable delay via `addDelayedHealthChecks()`.
